            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the boy from <a href="/wiki/Syrup_Village" title="Syrup Village">Syrup Village</a>, see <a href="/wiki/Ninjin" title="Ninjin">Ninjin</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Carrot</b> is a rabbit <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">mink</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Mokomo_Dukedom" title="Mokomo Dukedom">Mokomo Dukedom</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> the current ruler of the dukedom,<sup id="cite_ref-c1056_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1056-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-c1115_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1115-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> and a former member of the <a href="/wiki/Kingsbird" title="Kingsbird">Kingsbirds</a><sup id="cite_ref-Kingsbird_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kingsbird-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi_Musketeer_Squad" title="Inuarashi Musketeer Squad">Inuarashi Musketeer Squad</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Musketeer_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Musketeer-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> She was trained by <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a>, whose <a href="/wiki/Inherited_Will" title="Inherited Will">will</a> she carries on.
</p><p>She is an ally of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island_Saga" title="Whole Cake Island Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</a> and <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country Arc</a>, where she joined the Sanji Retrieval Team to rescue Sanji on <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island" title="Whole Cake Island">Whole Cake Island</a><sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> and participated in the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>. 
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Carrot is a white-furred, blonde-haired rabbit mink with brown eyes, rabbit ears, a rabbit-like nose, a large round fluffy tail, but with a body otherwise similar to that of a human adolescent girl. She is shorter than average, with a height of 161 cm (5'3").<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In her first appearance, she wore a short orange dress with laced-up open sides with the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a>' signature green cape,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> a single rabbit paw-like gauntlet, and brown, high-heeled boots.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> She wears this same outfit during the <a href="/wiki/Raid_on_Onigashima" title="Raid on Onigashima">Raid on Onigashima</a>. After becoming ruler, Carrot now wears a thicker, hooded version of her previous cape.<sup id="cite_ref-c1115_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1115-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon sneaking aboard the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, she changed to a similar short orange dress with the word "RABBIT" at the front with a thick darker orange trim and a single white stripe in the middle, a black cap, and yellow loafers.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> She also had a backpack and a canteen.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on, she was seen wearing another short orange dress with a puffy skirt and a hood, and retained her cap and loafers.
</p><p>After reaching <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>, Carrot donned a simple, light-green short-skirt dress decorated with three vertical stripes running down the center and frills at the bottom, neck, and sleeves, and tied up at the front with an orange bow, as well as a pair of orange dress shoes.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> An additional accessory includes an orange hat. 
</p><p>At the meeting with the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a>, she wore a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/flapper" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:flapper">flapper</a>-style outfit of a white cloche hat with a pink rose, a sleeveless white blouse with a frilly collar and pink ribbon, a frilly black skirt, and black pumps.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> Her outfit had different colors (yellow blouse, red skirt, and orange pumps) in the original "<a href="/wiki/Hope" title="Hope">Hope</a>" opening.
</p><p>At the start of the <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country_Arc" title="Wano Country Arc">Wano Country Arc</a>, she wore a simple short salmon pink halter dress with a carrot design and the word "Ninjin" (Japanese for "Carrot"), as well as frills at the bottom. After Kin'emon used <a href="/wiki/Fuku_Fuku_no_Mi" title="Fuku Fuku no Mi">his powers</a> to disguise her as a kunoichi, Carrot donned a light polka-dotted veil concealing her ears, a light green kimono with orange and green floral prints, and simple straw sandals.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Kin'emon used his Devil Fruit abilities again to disguise them, she wore a Beasts Pirates attire. Her outfit consists of a strapless green bikini armor, lighter green shoulder pads with white edges, and a furry magenta cape, however it appears black in the manga. 
</p><p>During the post-raid festival, she donned a short turquoise kimono with yellow floral patterns and a rose-pink obi.
</p><p>After being appointed ruler of the Mokomo Dukedom, Carrot wears a puffy coat with a bow.<sup id="cite_ref-c1115_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1115-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During her training under <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a>, she wore a red <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi_Musketeer_Squad" title="Inuarashi Musketeer Squad">musketeer</a> hat and a light-green dress with thin straps, and her hair was slightly shorter.
</p><p>When Carrot activates her Sulong form on a full moon, her eyes turn red with black sclera, her ears grow larger, her hair and tail grow considerably and turn snow white in color, and they both emit Electro sparks. The fur around her neckline turns much thicker, vaguely resembling a lion's mane, and her claws become longer and sharper. Upon seeing this form, <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> considers it to be "so beautiful." and <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> comments that "it's quite mesmerizing."
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Gallery">Gallery</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Carrot_Hope.png/revision/latest?cb=20181019205639" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Hope" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="61" height="105" data-image-name="Carrot Hope.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Hope.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7d/Carrot_Hope.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/61?cb=20181019205639" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Carrot's outfit as colored in the original <a href="/wiki/Hope" title="Hope">Hope</a> opening.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Carrot_Marine_Outfit.png/revision/latest?cb=20170328014834" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Marine Outfit" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="105" data-image-name="Carrot Marine Outfit.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Marine_Outfit.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Carrot_Marine_Outfit.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20170328014834" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Carrot's disguise during the <a href="/wiki/Marine_Rookie_Arc" title="Marine Rookie Arc">Marine Rookie Arc</a>.

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Carrot is very protective of the <a href="/wiki/Mokomo_Dukedom" title="Mokomo Dukedom">Mokomo Dukedom</a> and is highly aggressive towards intruders.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Like other minks, she refers to <a href="/wiki/Humans" title="Humans">humans</a> as "lesser minks".<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> Carrot is also protective of people she cares about. When the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> were met by <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>, Carrot was willing to fight the evil army in order to protect them.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> She can also be very emotional; when <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> ate poisonous fish skin and was left on the verge of death, Carrot begged him not to die and tearfully embraced him once the poison was sucked out of him.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> After <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> sacrificed himself in a suicidal explosion, Carrot became devastated and cried profoundly before becoming enraged to where she attempted to take it out on <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Katakuri</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png/revision/latest?cb=20201120172741" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Gnaws On Luffy&#39;s Ear" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Gnaws On Luffy&#39;s Ear.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201120172741" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png/revision/latest?cb=20201120172741" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Gnaws On Luffy&#39;s Ear" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201120172741" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Gnaws On Luffy&#39;s Ear.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/86/Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201120172741" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Gnaws_On_Luffy%27s_Ear.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot gnaws on Luffy's ear.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Like a regular rabbit, she likes to gnaw on things, including people such as Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> She loves carrots to the point where her provisions for the trip to <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island" title="Whole Cake Island">Whole Cake Island</a> consisted entirely of them, and she ferociously attacked Luffy when she saw him eating her carrot.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> She also loves chocolate.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Though feral and vicious when attacking someone, Carrot can be quickly calmed down if someone pats her head.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Despite her warrior status, she seems to be naive and childish about serious matters and the world beyond <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a>; she was easily excited by events new to her; when she heard Luffy was planning to crash <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>'s party and ruin the wedding ceremony, she believed it would be exciting to take part in, not realizing the extreme danger she would be facing in doing so,<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> and she was later surprised to hear that it would take several days to reach Whole Cake Island because of how big the ocean was, having believed that it was small enough to only warrant half a day's worth of provisions.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Additionally, she is not familiar with some natural weather phenomena, having mistaken lightning for <a href="/wiki/Electro" title="Electro">Electro</a> upon witnessing it at sea.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> She has always wanted to see the outside world and go on an adventure, and upon her discovery aboard the Thousand Sunny, she begged <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> not to take her home immediately out of fear of being berated by <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> She is apparently scared of ghosts as she was frightened by Brook's soul form.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite her naivete, she has also proven that she can be rather clever and deceiving; she quickly devised a plot to use <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">mirror based powers</a> against her and successfully fooled several <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> into thinking that they had captured her.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png/revision/latest?cb=20210626190342" class="image"><img alt="Sulong Carrot Blushing" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="172" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sulong Carrot Blushing.png" data-image-key="Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210626190342" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png/revision/latest?cb=20210626190342" class="image"><img alt="Sulong Carrot Blushing" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210626190342" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="172" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sulong Carrot Blushing.png" data-image-key="Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/68/Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210626190342" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sulong_Carrot_Blushing.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot blushing while in Sulong form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Whenever she transforms into her Sulong form, Carrot seemingly becomes more confident and vicious in combat. However, despite her drastic change in appearance and abilities, she still maintained her original personality, as shown when she blushed while fighting Charlotte Daifuku's crew. However, she proved to be more cunning than usual, as when she removed the steering wheel off of Daifuku's ship to keep them from going after the Sunny, and when she tricked his <a href="/wiki/Hoya_Hoya_no_Mi" title="Hoya Hoya no Mi">genie</a> into attacking its master's fleet.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Friends_and_Allies">Friends and Allies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Mink_Tribe">Mink Tribe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Carrot is loyal to her fellow minks and has a close friendship with <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a>. Though Wanda was initially worried when the minks could not find Carrot after the latter snuck onboard the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Wanda admitted that she was simply glad to know where she was.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Carrot, on the other hand, was afraid that Wanda would berate her if the Sanji Retrieval Team return to Zou, and pleaded <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> not to send her back. <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> had great faith in her, naming her their successor as ruler of the Mokomo Dukedom. Despite her youth and there being more experienced warriors, the entire tribe full-heartedly supported this choice, offering their power to help her rule.<sup id="cite_ref-c1056_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1056-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pedro">Pedro</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png/revision/latest?cb=20180819025333" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Gives Carrot Her Gauntlets" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="128" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pedro Gives Carrot Her Gauntlets.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180819025333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png/revision/latest?cb=20180819025333" class="image"><img alt="Pedro Gives Carrot Her Gauntlets" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180819025333" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="128" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pedro Gives Carrot Her Gauntlets.png" data-image-key="Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180819025333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pedro_Gives_Carrot_Her_Gauntlets.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Pedro gives Carrot her gauntlets.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Since her days training as a Musketeer, Carrot has looked up to Pedro despite his occupation as a <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardian</a>. He was even caring enough to gift her own gauntlets after witnessed her lack of talent for swordsmanship, and helped develop her combat prowess as her sparring partner. Their bond was even close enough for him to reiterate <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>'s advice as encouragement.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Carrot snuck aboard the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Pedro was worried about the danger she would be put in and asked to bring her back to Zou much to her own dismay. He ultimately vouched for her strength after Luffy agreed to let her stay.<sup id="cite_ref-c823_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c823-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before their escape, Pedro expressed his final thoughts to Carrot, having been convinced that the Straw Hats will be the ones to lead the <a href="/wiki/World" title="World">world</a> to its <a href="/wiki/Dawn_of_the_World" title="Dawn of the World">dawn</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> After telling Carrot she would understand the importance of helping the Straw Hats someday, Pedro made his sacrifice by detonating the explosives on his body in order to take out <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Perospero</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Straw_Hat_Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png/revision/latest?cb=20201102082412" class="image"><img alt="Sanji and Carrot Console Each Other" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji and Carrot Console Each Other.png" data-image-key="Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201102082412" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png/revision/latest?cb=20201102082412" class="image"><img alt="Sanji and Carrot Console Each Other" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201102082412" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji and Carrot Console Each Other.png" data-image-key="Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/98/Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20201102082412" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_and_Carrot_Console_Each_Other.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and Sanji console each other over Pedro's death.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Like the other minks, Carrot is grateful to the Straw <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Hats</a> for saving the citizens of Zou after they were devastated by <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>'s invasion. Carrot even joined the Sanji Retrieval Team in entering Big Mom's territory to rescue their captive crewmate and though they initially wanted to bring her back to Zou, they nonetheless allowed her to join. Carrot has become close to <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a>, giving him the nickname "Choniki"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">チョニキ</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> and the two worked together in defeating <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a>. Like the others, she was excited to hear <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> again and was bashful when they received praise from <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> in completing their assigned tasks.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> After the Sanji Retrieval Team escaped Totto Land, Carrot was overjoyed at the prospect of eating Sanji's food again.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Beasts_Pirates">Beasts Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>When Jack invaded Zou in search of Raizo, Carrot took a stand against his forces alongside the other minks. Like the rest of her tribe, she has sworn to never forgive Jack for destroying their country.
</p><p>As a member of the Ninja-Pirate-Mink-Samurai Alliance, Carrot is an enemy to the entire <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Family" title="Kurozumi Family">Kurozumi Family</a>, intending to assist the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> to overthrow them and restore <a href="/wiki/Wano_Country" title="Wano Country">Wano Country</a> to its former glory.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Big_Mom_Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Carrot became an enemy of Big Mom's family and crew during the mission to retrieve Sanji from Totto Land. At the Seducing Woods, she clashed against <a href="/wiki/Randolph" title="Randolph">Randolph</a>, who was sent to deal with the intruders. <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a> is also very antagonistic towards Carrot, saying that she wants to slice the latter's face because of how pretty it is.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> After imprisoning Carrot in the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>, Brûlée planned to put her in boiling soup, although this failed. She further earned the latter's fury by using her power to navigate through Big Mom's territory to find her friends. After <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> sacrificed himself in a suicidal explosion, Carrot was filled with sorrow and rage, to where she took it out on Katakuri. Carrot dealt a critical blow to <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> when she transformed and disabled his ship to prevent him from chasing the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Charlotte_Perospero">Charlotte Perospero</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Moon_Raid.png/revision/latest?cb=20220206042516" class="image"><img alt="Moon Raid" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Moon Raid.png" data-image-key="Moon_Raid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Moon_Raid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220206042516" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Moon_Raid.png/revision/latest?cb=20220206042516" class="image"><img alt="Moon Raid" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Moon_Raid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220206042516" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Moon Raid.png" data-image-key="Moon_Raid.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Moon_Raid.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20220206042516" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Moon_Raid.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and Wanda attack Perospero for Pedro's death.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Carrot holds a strong grudge against Perospero, as when Carrot saw that Perospero survived <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a>'s suicide attack, she was shocked and furious to see that he resisted her friend's sacrifice, and when Perospero guided Big Mom to walk the sea surface, she remained angry at him.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> When she discovered that Perospero was on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, she immediately made it her goal to track him down,<sup id="cite_ref-c992_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c992-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> and attacked him, despite his assertion that he had nothing to do with Pedro's choice to sacrifice himself.<sup id="cite_ref-c995_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c995-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Though even with <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a>'s help, the two were swiftly defeated upon losing their Sulong forms due to the clouds covering the full moon.<sup id="cite_ref-c1006_43-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> However, the two later witnessed <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> confronting Perospero,<sup id="cite_ref-c1023_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1023-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> and watch the full fight as Nekomamushi avenged Pedro's death by defeating Perospero personally.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Carrot has proven to be a strong warrior. Upon noticing that <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> was eating her carrot, an enraged Carrot quickly overwhelmed him before being calmed down, although this was an oversight on the part of the pirate<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>; this prompted <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a>, an extremely strong mink warrior and captain of the Guardians to vouch for her usefulness in a fight.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Carrot possesses a strong will as she was able to withstand a burst of Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Electro" title="Electro">Electro</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>As a mink, Carrot is a natural-born fighter<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> and can use Electro.<sup id="cite_ref-Electro_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Electro-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Having been a <a href="/wiki/Mokomo_Dukedom#Administration" title="Mokomo Dukedom">Kingsbird</a>, she possesses a large amount of stamina, which allows her to be active at all hours of the day.<sup id="cite_ref-Kingsbird_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kingsbird-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617193759" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Floats Over Zoro" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Floats Over Zoro.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617193759" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png/revision/latest?cb=20230617193759" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Floats Over Zoro" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617193759" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="136" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Floats Over Zoro.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4e/Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230617193759" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Floats_Over_Zoro.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot floats over Zoro's attack.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Carrot is immensely quick and agile, having effortlessly dodged a slash from <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Levitation_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Levitation-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> She is also capable of flipping backward multiple times and attacking immediately afterwards.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Carrot can levitate and jump in midair<sup id="cite_ref-Levitation_51-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Levitation-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> as well as jump extremely high.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> She is highly perceptive and has incredible reflexes, being able to notice <a href="/wiki/Randolph" title="Randolph">Randolph</a>'s extremely quick ambush before <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a> did, and managing to pull them out of harm's way a split second before Randolph attacked them.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Her immense speed is further shown when she instantly caught Diesel who is an extremely fast runner, despite him having a running start.
</p><p>Carrot is also physically very strong, as she is capable of carrying two large weights in her arms while still being able to run at the same time. She has incredible leg strength as she can topple a massive pot of boiling soup towards Brûlée with a kick. She is considerably durable, as she was able to sit back up after being stomped to the ground by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Charlotte Katakuri</a>, one of the Sweet Commanders of the Big Mom Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sulong_Form">Sulong Form</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Sulong" title="Sulong">Sulong</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png/revision/latest?cb=20171211211019" class="image"><img alt="Carrot&#39;s Sulong Transformation" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="164" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot&#39;s Sulong Transformation.png" data-image-key="Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171211211019" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png/revision/latest?cb=20171211211019" class="image"><img alt="Carrot&#39;s Sulong Transformation" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171211211019" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="164" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot&#39;s Sulong Transformation.png" data-image-key="Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c8/Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171211211019" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot%27s_Sulong_Transformation.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot transforms into her Sulong form.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a member of the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a>, Carrot is able to awaken the Sulong transformation when looking at the full moon. In this form, Carrot's strength, speed, agility, Electro, and fighting abilities are magnified, allowing her to take out multiple members of the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a> in the blink of an eye, and rip out the helm of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a>'s ship. Her gliding abilities have also improved, as she was able to glide from the crow's nest of the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> to Daifuku's ship a great distance away.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Using this form has a risk as it can cause severe exhaustion if used for too long.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> She can revert back to her normal form by blocking her eyes from moonlight.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Artistic_Skill">Artistic Skill</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Carrot%27s_Drawings.png/revision/latest?cb=20180114134053" class="image"><img alt="Carrot&#39;s Drawings" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot&#39;s Drawings.png" data-image-key="Carrot%27s_Drawings.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Carrot%27s_Drawings.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180114134053" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Carrot%27s_Drawings.png/revision/latest?cb=20180114134053" class="image"><img alt="Carrot&#39;s Drawings" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Carrot%27s_Drawings.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180114134053" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot&#39;s Drawings.png" data-image-key="Carrot%27s_Drawings.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/17/Carrot%27s_Drawings.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180114134053" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot%27s_Drawings.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot presents her artwork.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Carrot is skilled at drawing, but she has a tendency to draw people <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bish%C5%8Dnen" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bishōnen">very effeminately</a>. She is able to draw the faces of the Sanji Retrieval Team from memory.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> According to herself, she is also very good at drawing maps.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png/revision/latest?cb=20201120172815" class="image"><img alt="Carrot&#39;s Clawed Paw Gauntlet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot&#39;s Clawed Paw Gauntlet.png" data-image-key="Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201120172815" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png/revision/latest?cb=20201120172815" class="image"><img alt="Carrot&#39;s Clawed Paw Gauntlet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201120172815" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot&#39;s Clawed Paw Gauntlet.png" data-image-key="Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/06/Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20201120172815" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot%27s_Clawed_Paw_Gauntlet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot's clawed paw gauntlet.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Carrot wears two clawed gauntlets on her hands that resemble rabbit paws. They were given to her by Pedro when he believed that she could not handle a sword.<sup id="cite_ref-Claw_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Claw-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> They are strong enough to clash evenly with Zoro's swords and can have Electro channeled through them.<sup id="cite_ref-Electro_50-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Electro-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> When she encountered Luffy's group back when they first arrived on Zou, she wore a gauntlet only on her right hand.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>At some point in her youth, Carrot joined the <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi_Musketeer_Squad" title="Inuarashi Musketeer Squad">Inuarashi Musketeer Squad</a> and was trained in swordsmanship by <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a>. However, she lacked talent with the weapon, which caused <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a> to take her under his wing and give her a pair of gauntlets instead.<sup id="cite_ref-Claw_60-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Claw-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="During_the_Timeskip">During the Timeskip</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>When the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, attacked <a href="/wiki/Zou" title="Zou">Zou</a> in search of <a href="/wiki/Raizo" title="Raizo">Raizo</a>, Carrot and the rest of the Inuarashi Musketeer Squad fought against them until 6:00 PM, at which point <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a> ordered them to retreat so <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a> could take over the battle.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The battle against the Beast Pirates lasted for five days. On the fifth day of the battle, Jack lost his patience and unleashed <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Koro" title="Koro">Koro</a> gas, which left the <a href="/wiki/Mink_Tribe" title="Mink Tribe">Mink Tribe</a> poisoned and drastically weakened.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> 
<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Saga">Dressrosa Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Arc">Dressrosa Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The following day, Jack left Zou after hearing about <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>'s defeat and capture,<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> and the minks were later saved when <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> and his group came to Zou.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After <a href="/wiki/Capone_Bege" title="Capone Bege">Capone Bege</a> took Sanji and Caesar, Nekomamushi told Carrot and <a href="/wiki/Wanda" title="Wanda">Wanda</a> to keep quiet about the incident because that was what <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and her friends wanted.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zou_Arc">Zou Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Carrot saw <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Roronoa Zoro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</a> enter the <a href="/wiki/Mokomo_Dukedom" title="Mokomo Dukedom">Mokomo Dukedom</a> and, assuming that they had beaten the <a href="/wiki/Bariete" title="Bariete">guard</a> outside, rushed at them. Zoro attempted to attack her, but she evaded his strike before clashing with him. However, Wanda appeared and told Carrot to stop because they needed to deal with the intruder in the Whale Forest.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png/revision/latest?cb=20160626203409" class="image"><img alt="Wanda Takes Luffy to Right Belly Fortress" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Wanda Takes Luffy to Right Belly Fortress.png" data-image-key="Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160626203409" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png/revision/latest?cb=20160626203409" class="image"><img alt="Wanda Takes Luffy to Right Belly Fortress" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160626203409" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Wanda Takes Luffy to Right Belly Fortress.png" data-image-key="Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/4d/Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160626203409" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Wanda_Takes_Luffy_to_Right_Belly_Fortress.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and Wanda take Luffy to the Right Belly Fortress.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Shocked by this news, Carrot jumped high into the air to survey the situation and informed Wanda of the ongoing scuffle in the forest before joining her atop <a href="/wiki/Wany" title="Wany">Wany</a> and heading to the source of the disturbance. En route, Carrot learned that she had just attacked members of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> and noted that they were in for a shock. Shortly afterward, Carrot reached the Whale Forest with Wanda and calmed down <a href="/wiki/Roddy" title="Roddy">Roddy</a>, who was fighting with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, by giving him a fluttering cloth to attack.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> As she, Wanda, and Luffy rode on Wany through <a href="/wiki/Zunesha" title="Zunesha">Zunesha</a>'s self-washing deluge of seawater, Carrot explained how the twice-daily washing brought plenty of fish for the minks to eat before revealing that <a href="/wiki/Bepo" title="Bepo">Bepo</a> was under the care of Master Nekomamushi because he was a pirate as she bit on Luffy's ear. However, as they passed the crucifixes that Jack had used to torture some of the minks, Carrot quickly grew somber. After the other Straw Hats appeared, Carrot and the others arrived at Right Belly Fortress.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Carrot took part in a feast with the Straw Hats and several other minks, where she explained to Usopp that they refused to eat any meat from animals with fur.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> After the Straw Hats visited Inuarashi, Carrot and Wanda traveled with them to the Whale Forest to meet Nekomamushi.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
