<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png/revision/latest?cb=20161129124321" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Excited at Luffy&#39;s Plan" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="121" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Excited at Luffy&#39;s Plan.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161129124321" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png/revision/latest?cb=20161129124321" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Excited at Luffy&#39;s Plan" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161129124321" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="121" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Excited at Luffy&#39;s Plan.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161129124321" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Excited_at_Luffy%27s_Plan.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot expresses excitement at Luffy's plan to infiltrate Big Mom's territory.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once they arrived, Carrot and Wanda went with Luffy, Nami, and Pedro to see <a href="/wiki/Pekoms" title="Pekoms">Pekoms</a>, who was left behind by the <a href="/wiki/Big_Mom_Pirates" title="Big Mom Pirates">Big Mom Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Laughing at Luffy's proclamation that the Big Mom Pirates would become subordinate to him after he confronted <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Linlin" title="Charlotte Linlin">Big Mom</a>, Carrot was disturbed by Pekoms's explanation of what would happen if Sanji had refused Big Mom's invitation, only to become excited at the thought of helping Luffy interfere with Sanji's marriage ceremony, which prompted Wanda to reprimand her for taking it so lightly. Later, Carrot partied alongside the Straw Hats and other minks.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The following day, as Bariete rang the bell and spoke of the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Samurai" title="Samurai">samurais</a>, Carrot and the rest of the minks rushed to Kurau City. When <a href="/wiki/Kin%27emon" title="Kin&#39;emon">Kin'emon</a> and <a href="/wiki/Kurozumi_Kanjuro" title="Kurozumi Kanjuro">Kanjuro</a> revealed themselves, Carrot and the minks welcomed them and revealed that Raizo was on Zou before standing proudly at having kept his presence a secret.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> Kin'emon showed Carrot and the other minks the crest of the <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Family" title="Kouzuki Family">Kouzuki Family</a> on his back to confirm his allegiance. When Inuarashi and Nekomamushi reluctantly called a truce for the sake of <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Momonosuke" title="Kouzuki Momonosuke">Kouzuki Momonosuke</a>, whom they recognized as their lord, Carrot and the rest of the minks were overjoyed.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Inuarashi and Nekomamushi took Law, the Straw Hats, and the samurai to the Whale Tree, the minks discussed the day that the two rulers began hating each other, with Carrot noting that she had not even been born yet at the time. Happy that the two rulers finally made peace with each other, Carrot and the rest of the minks began to prepare a banquet to celebrate the occasion.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> However, when Inuarashi, Nekomamushi, the samurais, and the pirates returned from the Whale Tree with Raizo, Zou began shaking as Zunesha started crying out, throwing Carrot and the others into a state of panic.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> Jack had returned and was attempting to destroy Zou by killing Zunesha, who retaliated on Momonosuke's command and sank Jack's fleet with one blow, calming down Carrot and the others in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Wanting to go on an adventure, Carrot later went down to the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a> in secret in order to join the Sanji retrieval mission,<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> bribing Bariete with bananas not to tell anyone.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png/revision/latest?cb=20170301191203" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Joins Sanji Retrieval Team" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Joins Sanji Retrieval Team.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170301191203" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png/revision/latest?cb=20170301191203" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Joins Sanji Retrieval Team" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170301191203" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Joins Sanji Retrieval Team.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170301191203" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Joins_Sanji_Retrieval_Team.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot unexpectedly joins the Sanji retrieval team.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Carrot later revealed herself to the Sanji Retrieval Team after they had sailed far away from Zou, to their great surprise. As Carrot greeted everyone on the ship, Pedro tried to have the ship turned around so she could return to Zou, but Carrot begged them to let her come along and promised not to cause any trouble for the group. Luffy allowed her to come along because she was already on board, but despite her gratitude, Carrot immediately attacked him upon noticing that he was eating one of her carrots, only calming down when Luffy patted her head at Nami's behest.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Carrot and the rest of the Sanji Retrieval Team were surprised to learn of the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>' attack on the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary Army</a>'s headquarters on <a href="/wiki/Baltigo" title="Baltigo">Baltigo</a>. After the team passed through a storm, with Carrot mistaking lightning for <a href="/wiki/Electro" title="Electro">Electro</a>, Luffy presented his cooking, which Carrot and the group found to be completely inedible. Luffy then revealed that he had used up all of the food they had, leaving the team in a food shortage crisis.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marine_Rookie_Arc">Marine Rookie Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319183415" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats Eat at Fron Island" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hats Eat at Fron Island.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170319183415" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png/revision/latest?cb=20170319183415" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats Eat at Fron Island" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170319183415" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hats Eat at Fron Island.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/24/Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170319183415" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hats_Eat_at_Fron_Island.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and Luffy sneak into a Marine base to eat.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hungry from the lack of food on their voyage, Carrot was excited when the team approached <a href="/wiki/Fron_Island" title="Fron Island">Fron Island</a>, despite finding out it was home to a <a href="/wiki/Marine" class="mw-redirect" title="Marine">Marine</a> base. She, Luffy, Nami, Chopper, and Brook infiltrated the island, knocked some Marines unconscious, and stole their clothes. They then plotted to sneak into a food warehouse, but Carrot and Luffy walked into a cafeteria in the main base instead. They feasted on the food served to them, and when Nami and Chopper caught up to them, Carrot greeted them loudly, much to their chagrin. When Luffy's identity was discovered and broadcast by <a href="/wiki/Prodi" title="Prodi">Vice Admiral Prodi</a>, he and Carrot were confronted by the Marines in the cafeteria.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png/revision/latest?cb=20170327113604" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Shocks Zappa" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="194" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Shocks Zappa.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170327113604" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png/revision/latest?cb=20170327113604" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Shocks Zappa" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170327113604" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="194" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Shocks Zappa.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d5/Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170327113604" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Shocks_Zappa.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot knocks out Zappa with Electro.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Luffy noticed that he was surrounded by Marines, Carrot asked him what they should do, but Luffy couldn't care less about the Marines and instead replied that they should eat more, much to Carrot's surprise, but she joined Luffy anyway and ate more curry. After Luffy's brief scuffle with <a href="/wiki/All-Hunt_Grount" title="All-Hunt Grount">Grount</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ant_De_Bonham" title="Ant De Bonham">Bonham</a>, Carrot and Luffy fled the cafeteria. <a href="/wiki/Shimoi_Zappa" title="Shimoi Zappa">Zappa</a> stopped them in the hallway and, having taken a liking to Carrot, gave the rabbit mink a bouquet of carrots. Carrot then gave Zappa a garchu greeting, making him briefly faint from happiness. When Carrot and Luffy started running again, Zappa quickly got back on his feet and fought Luffy until he was subdued by Carrot's Electro. They then ran into Brook's soul form, which scared Carrot, and led them to the food storage house, defeating some Marine soldiers along the way.<sup id="cite_ref-Zappa_84-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zappa-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the food storage house, Carrot and the group gathered as much food as they can carry, but they were once again confronted by Grount, Bonham, and Zappa. After Carrot hit Zappa with another Electro, Zappa declared his love for both Nami and Carrot. In response, Nami used Thunder Breed Tempo on him. After exiting the storehouse with the food, they watched Luffy battling Grount. After Grount was overpowered, Carrot and her group prepared to depart the island. However, before they reached the Thousand Sunny, they were confronted by Vice Admiral Prodi.<sup id="cite_ref-Zappa_84-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Zappa-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The group tried to escape to the Submerge, but Prodi shot his bazooka at it before confronting them. The Sanji retrieval team dodged one of his bazooka blasts, and Carrot and Nami attacked the Marines but found that their electric attacks were unable to work against the Marines' rubber shields. However, they dispatched the Marines with physical attacks, and after Luffy defeated Prodi, Bonham, and Zappa, the team tried to escape to the still-intact Submerge. Luffy was confronted by Grount, and he told the group to go on ahead while he fought. Luffy eventually defeated Grount, and the group sailed away from Fron Island on the Thousand Sunny. However, the food they had stolen was eaten within 10 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Arc">Whole Cake Island Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>A few days later, Carrot and the rest of the group were famished from the lack of food and overheated as they passed through boiling waters but were saved from starvation when Luffy managed to catch a gigantic fish. After Luffy succumbed to food poisoning due to eating the fish's toxic skin, Carrot and the others enjoyed a meal prepared by Nami using Sanji's recipe. As they entered Big Mom's territory, the group was approached by a ship belonging to <a href="/wiki/Germa_66" title="Germa 66">Germa 66</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Upon seeing a hooded man aboard the ship, Carrot mistook him for Sanji until he revealed himself to be Sanji's younger brother, <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Yonji" title="Vinsmoke Yonji">Vinsmoke Yonji</a>, which Carrot was shocked at Nami deducing. As Luffy's condition worsened, Yonji refused to provide any aid and taunted the group to try to take the antidote by force, prompting Carrot to tearfully note that he was nowhere near as kind as Sanji was. When Sanji's older sister, <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Reiju" title="Vinsmoke Reiju">Vinsmoke Reiju</a>, appeared aboard the Thousand Sunny, Carrot angrily demanded to know who she was, only to watch in shock as Reiju sucked the poison out of Luffy's body, saving his life. With Carrot and Chopper overjoyed at Luffy's recovery, the Vinsmoke siblings and their men departed without reporting the Sanji Retrieval Team's presence.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png/revision/latest?cb=20170430181036" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team in Pudding&#39;s Home" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="126" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team in Pudding&#39;s Home.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170430181036" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png/revision/latest?cb=20170430181036" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team in Pudding&#39;s Home" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170430181036" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="126" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team in Pudding&#39;s Home.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/9e/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170430181036" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_Retrieval_Team_in_Pudding%27s_Home.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team as guests in Pudding's home.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The group later docked at <a href="/wiki/Cacao_Island" title="Cacao Island">Cacao Island</a>, an island close to <a href="/wiki/Whole_Cake_Island" title="Whole Cake Island">Whole Cake Island</a>, and Carrot and Nami changed into new outfits. When Carrot noticed people from different races living on the island, Pekoms explained Big Mom's dream of creating a nation where people from all races can live together. Seeing buildings made from chocolate, Carrot asked if the chocolate could be eaten, prompting Pekoms to reveal that it is illegal to consume the roofs because they protect residents against the precipitation the island receives. She and the rest of the Sanji Retrieval Team witnessed Luffy and Chopper getting into trouble for eating a café and subsequently being saved by the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Pudding" title="Charlotte Pudding">Charlotte Pudding</a>, who came to their defense. After Pudding bailed out Luffy and Chopper, Carrot and the team accompanied her to her home, where she fed them.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Carrot and the rest of the team discovered that Pudding was Sanji's betrothed, and Pudding told them how she met Sanji and became attracted to him, which caused Carrot to quickly warm up to her because of their shared admiration for him. After Pudding gave them a route to Whole Cake Island and promised to bring Sanji to them, the team left Pudding's home in a hurry when guards came for her. Upon returning to the Thousand Sunny, they discovered that Pekoms had gone missing and there was a message in the bathroom telling them to turn back.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest?cb=20160620215707" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160620215707" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest?cb=20160620215707" class="image"><img alt="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160620215707" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sanji Retrieval Team Battles a Centipede.png" data-image-key="Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c5/Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160620215707" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Battles_a_Centipede.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team battles a centipede at sea.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After leaving Cacao Island, Carrot and the rest of the team sailed through Pudding's route. Carrot and Chopper were excited when they approached the next <a href="/wiki/Jam_Island" title="Jam Island">island</a> on the route, but Nami decided not to dock at it. After asking to help with lookout duty, Carrot saw a grape-colored part of the ocean, which prompted Pedro to reveal that there were juice rivers coming from the islands. Suddenly, a giant sea centipede attacked the ship, and Carrot began to battle it alongside Luffy, Pedro, and Brook.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later, Carrot and the team battled a swarm of giant ants as night fell, and consequently got stuck in a frozen sea of syrup. As they worked to melt the syrup, Luffy asked Pedro about his previous experience in <a href="/wiki/Totto_Land" title="Totto Land">Totto Land</a>, which prompted Carrot to reveal that Pedro was once a pirate who sailed with Pekoms. Pedro explained his pirating history and how he met his defeat in Totto Land, which Carrot did not know about. The next morning, the team arrived at Whole Cake Island, which Carrot was excited to see.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Pedro and <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> departed to find Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">Road Poneglyph</a>, and Carrot, Luffy, Nami, and Chopper went ashore to look for Sanji and Pudding. Carrot, Luffy, and Chopper saw what appeared to be Sanji leaning against a tree, but to their surprise, he disappeared. They entered the Seducing Woods to look for Sanji but were frequently distracted by the sweets making up their surroundings. They were nearly eaten by a <a href="/wiki/Noble_Croc" title="Noble Croc">talking crocodile</a>, but it walked away when it saw that most of them were humans. Suddenly, Luffy confronted a <a href="/wiki/Mira_Mira_no_Mi" title="Mira Mira no Mi">reflection of himself</a>, shocking Carrot, Nami, and Chopper. Carrot thought she saw Sanji lying on a tree branch, but this version of him disappeared as well, and everyone except Luffy chased after a fleeing figure. After running into a <a href="/wiki/Pound" title="Pound">large man</a> buried up to his head, they were suddenly attacked by a <a href="/wiki/Randolph" title="Randolph">rabbit</a> riding a bird, and as everyone was thrown into chaos, everything in the forest came to life to trap and kill the pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png/revision/latest?cb=20170611020623" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Attacks Randolph" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="128" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Attacks Randolph.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170611020623" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png/revision/latest?cb=20170611020623" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Attacks Randolph" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170611020623" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="128" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Attacks Randolph.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/90/Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170611020623" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Attacks_Randolph.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot clashes with Randolph.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Carrot, Chopper, and Nami ran, Randolph continued to pursue them. Carrot informed them that despite Randolph's appearance, he was not a mink. She then clashed with Randolph and used Electro against him, which he was unable to do, confirming her words. Carrot then knocked out the crane he was riding on. Randolph then leaped off the crane and hurled its spear at the pirates, who managed to dodge the projectile, which struck the buried large man instead. They went back to the two Luffys and the fake Luffy went with them while the real Luffy ran in the opposite direction. They tried to escape the Seducing Woods, but they kept running into the buried large man. The Sanji Retrieval Team got lost in the mirrored woods, and the Luffy accompanying them revealed herself to be the reflection, transforming back into her true form, <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e" title="Charlotte Brûlée">Charlotte Brûlée</a>. She then grabbed Nami and prepared to slice her and Carrot's faces.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest?cb=20171117162455" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Traps Carrot" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="274" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Brûlée Traps Carrot.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171117162455" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest?cb=20171117162455" class="image"><img alt="Brûlée Traps Carrot" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171117162455" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="274" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Brûlée Traps Carrot.png" data-image-key="Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/77/Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171117162455" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e_Traps_Carrot.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot trapped within Brûlée's mirror.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Nami used her <a href="/wiki/Art_of_Weather/Sorcery_Clima-Tact" title="Art of Weather/Sorcery Clima-Tact">Clima-Tact</a> to escape Brûlée's grasp, Carrot attempted to attack Brûlée using her "Eleclaw" technique, but Brûlée used her Devil Fruit power to reflect Carrot's attack back at her. Carrot tried to attack again, but Brûlée used her ability to trap Carrot into the <a href="/wiki/Mirro-World" title="Mirro-World">Mirro-World</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> Sometime later, Carrot was joined by Chopper. When Brûlée arrived at the scene where <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Cracker" title="Charlotte Cracker">Charlotte Cracker</a> was confronting Luffy and Nami, she smashed the mirror that Carrot and Chopper were trapped in. However, the two prisoners remained unharmed.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Inside the Mirro-World, a shackled Chopper told Carrot, also shackled, that he had a plan, and so she should call him "Brother Chopper". Carrot referred to him as "Choniki" and asked what the plan was. Chopper explained his realization that the Mirro-World is connected to every mirror on Whole Cake Island. Thus, instead of trying to escape, they should use Brûlée's power against her.<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Eleven hours later, Carrot and Chopper were running from Brûlée inside the Mirro-World, but began to grow tired.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> As they ran, Carrot and Chopper contacted Nami through a mirror shard and told her not to worry. However, their conversation ended abruptly.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest?cb=20171119162951" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Defeats Brûlée" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Defeats Brûlée.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171119162951" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest?cb=20171119162951" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Defeats Brûlée" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171119162951" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Defeats Brûlée.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d0/Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20171119162951" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Defeats_Br%C3%BBl%C3%A9e.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot kicks a pot of soup at Brûlée, defeating her.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Eventually, Brûlée caught them,<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> but Carrot and Chopper managed to acquire a frog that Brûlée had turned into a body double of Carrot with her powers. They tricked Brûlée into believing that the frog was Carrot, and Carrot followed them back to Brûlée's house, hiding in the attic and making cries of distress to continue the act. As Brûlée and her entourage prepared to lower the frog into a giant pot of boiling soup, Carrot threw a rock at Randolph before he could drop the frog into the pot. In the confusion, she then jumped down and kicked the pot at Brûlée, dousing her in the boiling soup and defeating her. Randolph and his comrades raced to help Brûlée, but Carrot cleverly used Electro on the soup, electrocuting all of them. <a href="/wiki/Diesel" title="Diesel">Diesel</a> ran away to report the incident to Big Mom, but Carrot chased him down and put her hands over his eyes, causing him to crash. Carrot and Chopper then celebrated their victory and prepared to use the mirror world to visit their allies.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png/revision/latest?cb=20240720170628" class="image"><img alt="Chopper and Carrot Traverse the Mirro-World" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Chopper and Carrot Traverse the Mirro-World.png" data-image-key="Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170628" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png/revision/latest?cb=20240720170628" class="image"><img alt="Chopper and Carrot Traverse the Mirro-World" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170628" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Chopper and Carrot Traverse the Mirro-World.png" data-image-key="Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d6/Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170628" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Chopper_and_Carrot_Traverse_the_Mirro-World.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and Chopper look for their teammates in Mirro-World.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With Brûlée as their prisoner, Carrot and Chopper raced through the Mirro-World using Diesel to find Luffy and the others.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Carrot managed to revive Brûlée by tickling her, and Brûlée revealed that the mirrors could talk to them. Carrot and Chopper asked the mirrors about their teammates, but the mirrors did not know what they looked like, so Carrot prepared to draw portraits of them.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> Carrot and Chopper located Pedro and made a plan for him to end his battle with <a href="/wiki/Tamago" title="Tamago">Tamago</a>. As Pedro blew up a large amount of explosives inside his jacket, Carrot and Chopper pulled him into the Mirro-World. As they continued traveling in the Mirro-World, Carrot and Chopper were informed of Luffy and Nami's capture but were later told by the mirrors that Nami was with <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> They located Nami and Jinbe and helped them escaped their pursuers by pulling them into the Mirro-World. With Nami and Jinbe in the group, the team went on searching for Luffy, Brook, and Sanji.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Carrot's group located Brook inside Big Mom's bedroom, being held in her hands as she slept. Brûlée tried to alert her mother, causing the team to bind and gag her and Diesel. Upon witnessing Big Mom and her three <a href="/wiki/Homies" title="Homies">homies</a> attacking a fly, the team became terrified, wondering how they were supposed to save Brook. The team then made a skeletal lookalike for Brook, which they planned to use to make a stand-in for the real Brook. After Chopper's unsuccessful attempt to retrieve Brook, Carrot tried next, quietly landing on Big Mom before whispering to Brook to wake up. However, she was forced to flee from a sleep bubble coming from Big Mom's nose, and <a href="/wiki/Zeus" title="Zeus">Zeus</a> spotted her. Thinking she was the fly, Zeus shot a lightning bolt at Carrot. After Jinbe and Nami rescued Brook from Big Mom's clutches, the team was surprised to see that Brook successfully copied the <a href="/wiki/Poneglyph" title="Poneglyph">poneglyphs</a> and hid the copies inside his skull. The team then celebrated Brook's accomplishment.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20180304023006" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180304023006" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20180304023006" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180304023006" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hat Pirates Meet Fire Tank Pirates.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/58/Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180304023006" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hat_Pirates_Meet_Fire_Tank_Pirates.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team forms an alliance with the Fire Tank Pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The group searched for Sanji and Luffy, but none of the mirrors saw them inside the castle. Nami then theorized where Sanji and Luffy may be at and Carrot was surprised to hear that the two had a fight.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> Carrot's group later contacted Luffy and Sanji through a mirror shard and were surprised when Luffy decided to ruin the wedding ceremony. Carrot then listened as Jinbe explained more about the situation they were in, about Bege, his backstory, his plot against Big Mom and his suggestion to form an alliance.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup> After Luffy agreed to meet with the <a href="/wiki/Fire_Tank_Pirates" title="Fire Tank Pirates">Fire Tank Pirates</a> to form an alliance to take down Big Mom, Carrot and her group arrived at Bege's hideout before Luffy and Sanji. After taking a bath with Nami, she accompanied her team inside the meeting room where an argument broke out among Luffy, Caesar, and Bege until Jinbe settled it.<sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> As Bege explained his plan to kill Big Mom, Carrot listened attentively. The meeting adjourned once Bege finished going over the plan.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Bege transported the alliance members to the wedding inside his body. Before Bege walked into the wedding venue, Carrot was shown sleeping.<sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> After the wedding ceremony began, the team initially encountered a small problem when Jinbe had difficulty waking Luffy up. After they woke Luffy with meat, the team went into the Mirro-World and prepared to charge into the venue. Once they heard the signal, the team unleashed duplicates of Luffy into the venue, causing chaos at the ceremony.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup> After releasing all the duplicates, the team charged in. Carrot, Nami, and Chopper then hid inside the ruined wedding cake, waiting for the photo of <a href="/wiki/Carmel" title="Carmel">Mother Carmel</a> to be destroyed. They then watched in amazement as Jinbe without fear officially declared to Big Mom his intention to leave the Big Mom Pirates in order to join the Straw Hat Pirates and that Luffy would become the Pirate King.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> Three seconds after Brook destroyed Carmel's portrait, Carrot, Nami, and Chopper were confused as to why Big Mom did not already start screaming. However, they were later told by Bege to put on their earplugs as he initiated his assassination operation.<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest?cb=20180506042309" class="image"><img alt="Nami and Carrot Defend the Vinsmokes" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nami and Carrot Defend the Vinsmokes.png" data-image-key="Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180506042309" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest?cb=20180506042309" class="image"><img alt="Nami and Carrot Defend the Vinsmokes" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180506042309" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nami and Carrot Defend the Vinsmokes.png" data-image-key="Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180506042309" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nami_and_Carrot_Defend_the_Vinsmokes.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and Nami help Sanji rescue his family.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once Luffy caused Big Mom to start her strange scream, Carrot's group came out of hiding and assisted Sanji in rescuing the <a href="/wiki/Vinsmoke_Family" title="Vinsmoke Family">Vinsmoke Family</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> Carrot then watched as Bege, <a href="/wiki/Vito" title="Vito">Vito</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Gotti" title="Gotti">Gotti</a> fired their <a href="/wiki/KX_Launcher" title="KX Launcher">KX Launchers</a> at Big Mom. However, Big Mom's scream detonated the rockets before they could reach her. With the assassination attempt a failure, Caesar flew into the venue with the escape mirror and Bege signaled the alliance members to retreat. Before they could escape into the mirror, Big Mom's scream shattered it, leaving them trapped in the venue. After Bege transformed into <a href="/wiki/Shiro_Shiro_no_Mi" title="Shiro Shiro no Mi">Big Father</a>, he instructed the alliance to retreat inside.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> Before she could do so, Carrot watched as Nami was caught by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Smoothie" title="Charlotte Smoothie">Smoothie</a>, before being restrained herself by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Daifuku</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Hoya_Hoya_no_Mi" title="Hoya Hoya no Mi">genie</a>. However, she was released after Yonji attacked the genie. Carrot then retreated successfully into Bege's fortress, along with the rest of the alliance. However, they found themselves in a dire situation as Big Mom began attacking the fortress.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As Bege's fortress continued to suffer damage from Big Mom's attacks, Luffy attempted to fight back only to be reminded they have achieved their goals. Carrot then listened to Bege as he came up with a plan to escape with Caesar's help, and also when Sanji demanded his father to never appear before him and his friends ever again.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> Just when the Big Mom Pirates routed the Straw Hats, the Fire Tanks, and the Vinsmokes, the <a href="/wiki/Tamatebako" title="Tamatebako">Tamatebako</a> dropped to the base of the Whole Cake Chateau and exploded, causing the castle to topple over.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> As the castle collapsed, Carrot's group, Bege's crew, and the Vinsmoke Family got away. Carrot's group and the Fire Tank Pirates rendezvous at the northwest part of Whole Cake Island, where Bege decided to part ways with the Straw Hats.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest?cb=20170821042718" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170821042718" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest?cb=20170821042718" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170821042718" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hats Clash in the Seducing Woods.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/22/Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20170821042718" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hats_Clash_in_the_Seducing_Woods.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team clashes with the Big Mom Pirates while escaping.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Brook and Chopper separated from the group to retrieve the <a href="/wiki/Shark_Submerge_III" title="Shark Submerge III">Shark Submerge III</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup> the rest head for the Thousand Sunny. As they approached the Seducing Woods, they ran into <a href="/wiki/Kingbaum" title="Kingbaum">Kingbaum</a>. Nami then used part of Big Mom's <a href="/wiki/Vivre_Card" title="Vivre Card">Vivre Card</a> to control Kingbaum and forced him to transport the fleeing team. However, before they reached the Seducing Woods, a crazed Big Mom (while riding on Zeus) caught up to them.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> Using <a href="/wiki/Napoleon" title="Napoleon">Napoleon</a> in its sword form, Big Mom unleashed an air slash that cut off a part of Kingbaum. As Big Mom prepared to attack again, Nami diverted Zeus' attention by using thunderclouds, causing the cloud homie to veer off-course and drop Big Mom. When Carrot and her group reached the Seducing Woods, Big Mom ordered the tree homies to stop the Straw Hats, but Kingbaum charged through them. Carrot and her group were later forced to jump off Kingbaum when <a href="/wiki/Prometheus" title="Prometheus">Prometheus</a> attacked and burned Kingbaum for his betrayal.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the Sanji Retrieval Team continued with their escape, Big Mom resumed her pursuit. Thanks to Big Mom's presence, the Vivre Card in Nami's possession was rendered useless, and the Seducing Woods homies went to work attacking the Straw Hats and changing the landscape to confuse them. Several Big Mom Pirates caught up to their captain and clashed with the Sanji Retrieval Team. Along the way, Luffy stopped Carrot from separating from the group. The team pulled out of the conflict quickly, knowing they could not split up there. When Zeus ate one of Nami's weather eggs and grew massively and became stormy, Nami took the opportunity to summon a massive lightning bolt that struck the Big Mom Pirates pursuing them.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nami's attack left Big Mom laying at the bottom of a crater. To the Straw Hats' shock, Big Mom was barely affected and continued to move. She ate through the ground as she moved back up, and the team started running again. They were then approached by Pudding and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Chiffon" title="Charlotte Chiffon">Chiffon</a>. After Chiffon requested Sanji's help in making a cake for Big Mom, Sanji readily agreed to assist them. Big Mom then got back on her feet and unleashed another devastating air slash, and the two groups parted ways, with Sanji heading to Cacao Island with Pudding and Chiffon while Carrot and her group continued fleeing to the Thousand Sunny. Pudding used <a href="/wiki/Memo_Memo_no_Mi" title="Memo Memo no Mi">her Devil Fruit powers</a> to send memories flooding into the souls in the homies, allowing the Straw Hats to make it to the coast without trouble.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png/revision/latest?cb=20180822045619" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Subdues Carrot" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="169" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Katakuri Subdues Carrot.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180822045619" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png/revision/latest?cb=20180822045619" class="image"><img alt="Katakuri Subdues Carrot" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180822045619" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="169" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Katakuri Subdues Carrot.png" data-image-key="Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20180822045619" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Katakuri_Subdues_Carrot.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot is subdued by Katakuri.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>They ran toward the Sunny and came into conflict with <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Perospero" title="Charlotte Perospero">Perospero</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Katakuri" title="Charlotte Katakuri">Katakuri</a>, who were already on board. Pedro told Carrot not to be flustered by these events, as he believed that the Straw Hats would bring about the <a href="/wiki/Dawn_of_the_World" title="Dawn of the World">dawn of the world</a>. After Perospero trapped the Sunny in <a href="/wiki/Pero_Pero_no_Mi" title="Pero Pero no Mi">candy</a>, Carrot watched in shock as Pedro attempted to take out Perospero with a massive suicidal explosion.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup> Carrot then cried out and was about to go to the coast to get Pedro. Nami stopped her from leaving the ship, saying that they could not afford to waste the chance that Pedro provided them. Carrot then tried to attack Katakuri, but the Sweet Commander easily subdued her. After Luffy grabbed Katakuri and dragged him into the Mirro-World, Carrot and her group on the Thousand Sunny successfully escaped Whole Cake Island with a Coup de Burst.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the team mourned Pedro's self-sacrifice and lamented on their inability to save him, Jinbe encouraged them to press on and keep their guard up. As the team was spurred into action, Carrot jumped up to the crow's nest and saw not only the Big Mom Pirates' fleet heading toward them but Big Mom herself, who was walking on water using Perospero's candy road. Upon seeing Perospero standing on top of Big Mom, Carrot gazed at him with a furious expression.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Plan_to_Meet_at_Cacao_Island.png/revision/latest?cb=20230209020133" class="image"><img alt="The Sanji Retrieval Team Plan to Meet at Cacao Island" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="189" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Sanji Retrieval Team Plan to Meet at Cacao Island.png" data-image-key="The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Plan_to_Meet_at_Cacao_Island.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Plan_to_Meet_at_Cacao_Island.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230209020133" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/7b/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Plan_to_Meet_at_Cacao_Island.png/revision/latest?cb=20230209020133" class="image"><img alt="The Sanji Retrieval Team Plan to Meet at Cacao Island" loading="lazy" width="210" height="189" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Sanji Retrieval Team Plan to Meet at Cacao Island.png"
