	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Plan_to_Meet_at_Cacao_Island.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team plan their next move.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While under siege by the Big Mom Pirates, Carrot informed Nami of another predicament, which was Big Mom creating a massive wave homie to engulf the Thousand Sunny.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> As the wave homie got closer, Carrot apologized to Pedro how she and her friends would not be able to escape even after his sacrifice, but thanks to Jinbe's skills as a <a href="/wiki/Helmsman" title="Helmsman">helmsman</a>, the team managed to come out of that situation unharmed. They then contacted Luffy through a mirror shard and told him to find a mirror connecting to <a href="/wiki/Cacao_Island" title="Cacao Island">Cacao Island</a> so they could meet him there.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On the way to Cacao Island, the group on the Sunny was puzzled when they saw no pursuers. Carrot and Chopper kept a vigilant lookout.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> As they were getting near Cacao Island, Carrot noted that a full moon was coming.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20181118035347" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Attacks Daifuku&#39;s Fleet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Carrot Attacks Daifuku&#39;s Fleet.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181118035347" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png/revision/latest?cb=20181118035347" class="image"><img alt="Carrot Attacks Daifuku&#39;s Fleet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181118035347" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Carrot Attacks Daifuku&#39;s Fleet.png" data-image-key="Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/97/Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20181118035347" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Carrot_Attacks_Daifuku%27s_Fleet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot activates her Sulong form and attacks the Big Mom Pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The group on the Sunny was later surprised to find themselves once again pursued by Big Mom and a fleet of Tarteships.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> They were initially able to hold their own, but they later discovered another fleet of Tarteships led by <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Daifuku" title="Charlotte Daifuku">Charlotte Daifuku</a> in front of them. As they were about to be surrounded by the Big Mom Pirates, they thought about a counterattack. Carrot told the rest of the team to leave this to her, and she activated her Sulong form by the power of the full moon. She swooped down and glided toward Daifuku's ship, where she rapidly attacked several Big Mom Pirates who could not keep up with her movements. She then went to the helm and destroyed it, preventing Daifuku's crew from piloting it.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> Enraged at Carrot's actions, Daifuku summoned a genie to attack Carrot. Carrot dodged the genie's strikes, causing it to damage the ships in Daifuku's fleet instead. Carrot continued her attack by destroying the helms of the other ships. Just when she was feeling fatigued from using the Sulong form, Brook arrived and grabbed her. Carrot then blocked her eyes from the moonlight and returned to her original form as Brook carried her back to the Thousand Sunny.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> Carrot rested inside the Sunny as the rest of the team fought against Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the Sunny was pursued by Smoothie's fleet after the Fire Tank Pirates lured Big Mom away, Carrot recovered from her exhaustion. She then asked the rest of the Sunny group if Luffy had won his battle.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> As the promised rendezvous time drew near, Nami pointed out that Luffy needed Brûlée in order to leave the Mirro-World, causing the group to become concerned, given Luffy's absent-mindedness. With a few minutes remaining, Cacao Island was in sight.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As the Sunny group sailed past the port of Cacao Island, they were overjoyed to see Sanji and Luffy coming towards them.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup> Luffy and Sanji returned to the Sunny and the group quickly made their retreat from Cacao Island. The group was then besieged by Smoothie's fleet, but Judge came to their rescue. After the Sunny passed by Judge's castle, the group later saw enemy ships approaching them from the front and Daifuku tried to attack Carrot with his genie, but Sanji blocked it. When the situation grew more dire, they were surprised when Wadatsumi appeared and attacked the enemy.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Sun Pirates cleared a path for the Sunny. However, despite their efforts, the Sunny was intercepted and attacked by the Queen Mama Chanter.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup> Wadatsumi saved the Sunny by switching it with the Sun Pirates' ship and hid the Sunny in his mouth. Wadatsumi tried swimming away, but Oven attacked him with heatwaves, forcing him to spit out the Sunny. As the Sun Pirates held back the Big Mom Pirates, Jinbe decided to stay behind to help them and Luffy consented to his decision. After Jinbe joined his former crew in battle, the Sunny group sailed far away from Cacao Island.<sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After escaping from Totto Land, Sanji learned about Pedro's self-sacrifice and expressed some regrets. Carrot tried to cheer Sanji up but ended up crying, prompting Sanji to comfort her. Later, the group on the Sunny happily waited for Sanji's cooking.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Levely_Arc">Levely Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6d/Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png/revision/latest?cb=20191128175134" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats React to Bounty" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="132" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Straw Hats React to Bounty.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6d/Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191128175134" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6d/Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png/revision/latest?cb=20191128175134" class="image"><img alt="Straw Hats React to Bounty" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6d/Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191128175134" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="132" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Straw Hats React to Bounty.png" data-image-key="Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6d/Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20191128175134" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Straw_Hats_React_to_Bounty.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and the Straw Hat Pirates shocked after seeing Luffy's new reward.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Carrot received a new newspaper and showed it to the group. They looked at the new bounty posters for Sanji and Luffy and the group was shocked to learn that Luffy's bounty increased to <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>1,500,000,000.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup>
<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the Thousand Sunny continued towards Wano Country, the group was informed of the Levely through a newspaper. They later encountered an unusual weather disturbance in their direction, followed by an octopus on their ship as well as a school of huge carp on their side. After a bumpy ride across a river, the ship climbed up a waterfall. Once they reached the top, they came across a whirlpool.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup> Sanji carried Nami, Chopper, Carrot, and Brook away from the ship, but Luffy got dragged into the whirlpool along with the Sunny.<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Luffy got separated, the group searched for him, but they only found his Vivre Card. They later got in touch with Kin'emon and they reunited with Luffy at the ruins of Oden Castle. With Law, Momonosuke, and Kiku also present, Kin'emon explained how he and his group traveled through time to escape Orochi's attack twenty years ago.<sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup> Carrot then listened as Kin'emon explained more about the past such as the story of Oden, the time of his execution, the rumor about Toki, and what Kin'emon's group did right after arriving at the present time. Kin'emon then went over a plan to attack Onigashima, the island where Kaidou resided, in two weeks.<sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png/revision/latest?cb=20240720170812" class="image"><img alt="The Sanji Retrieval Team Receives Clothing For Wano" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="188" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Sanji Retrieval Team Receives Clothing For Wano.png" data-image-key="The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170812" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png/revision/latest?cb=20240720170812" class="image"><img alt="The Sanji Retrieval Team Receives Clothing For Wano" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170812" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="188" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Sanji Retrieval Team Receives Clothing For Wano.png" data-image-key="The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/da/The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240720170812" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Sanji_Retrieval_Team_Receives_Clothing_For_Wano.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Sanji Retrieval Team receives appropriate clothing for Wano thanks to Kin'emon's powers.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Kin'emon explained more about the Fire Festival and how the decisive battle would play out. He then gave the group specific tasks to do. He asked Carrot and Chopper to go with Kiku to Inuarashi's current location. After giving the group new clothes, he introduced them to <a href="/wiki/Shinobu" title="Shinobu">Shinobu</a>. When Kaidou arrived at Kuri, Law alerted the group.<sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup> The group was surprised to see Kaidou and they learned that Luffy, Zoro, and Law were already exposed. Luffy rushed off to protect <a href="/wiki/Kuri#Okobore_Town" title="Kuri">Okobore Town</a> and Law chased after him and told the rest to remain unseen. After Kin'emon and Kiku left to rescue Tsuru, the rest at Oden Castle noticed Kaidou coming to their direction and tried to flee as Kaidou destroyed the castle with a fire breath.<sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> Sanji carried Carrot and Nami away while Shinobu saved the rest by using her Devil Fruit power to sink them into the ground. Kiku then returned and told them what happened to Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At Mt. Atamayama, Carrot witnessed <a href="/wiki/Ashura_Doji" title="Ashura Doji">Ashura Doji</a>'s clash with Inuarashi. After Kin'emon broke up the fight, Carrot was amazed that Ashura was an even match for Inuarashi.<sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup> Sometime later, Carrot and the Musketeers stole food and weapons from the Beasts Pirates and left a note saying that Ashura and his gang were responsible for the thefts.<sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At an abandoned village in Kuri, Carrot panicked after hearing that the Beasts Pirates found out about Kin'emon's secret message.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Prior to the raid on <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a>, Carrot, Wanda, and Shishilian were later at the place where graves for Pedro and <a href="/wiki/Shimotsuki_Yasuie" title="Shimotsuki Yasuie">Yasuie</a> were placed.<sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup> In Amigasa Village, Carrot marveled at the new armor Luffy, Brook, and Chopper received. After Robin stated that Onigashima's entrance is in winter, Carrot explained to the group that the seasons are not consistent in Wano and cold climate would give the minks an advantage.<sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png/revision/latest?cb=20240618215034" class="image"><img alt="Jinbe Rejoins Crew" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Jinbe Rejoins Crew.png" data-image-key="Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240618215034" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png/revision/latest?cb=20240618215034" class="image"><img alt="Jinbe Rejoins Crew" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240618215034" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Jinbe Rejoins Crew.png" data-image-key="Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/8/82/Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240618215034" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Jinbe_Rejoins_Crew.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and the straw hats excited to see Jinbe again.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the day of the Fire Festival, Carrot joined the Straw Hats on the Thousand Sunny as they entered the battle with the Beasts Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup> Kanjuro fled the scene with Momonosuke in tow on a drawn crane and briefly attacked the alliance with an ink cloud that rained down ink arrows. Momonosuke ordered the alliance to press forward to Onigashima without worrying about him. As the alliance was attacked by a Beasts Pirates ship with long ranged cannons, Jinbe came to aid the rebels. Like the Straw Hats, Carrot was also happy to see Jinbe again.<sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the Straw Hats defeated the guards at the torii gates, the alliance arrived at Onigashima.<sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup> After disembarking, Carrot received a Beasts Pirates disguise from Kin'emon. She then joined Chopper, Usopp, Nami, and Shinobu in the <a href="/wiki/Brachio_Tank_V" title="Brachio Tank V">Brachio Tank V</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup> The group in the tank and Kin'emon's forces reached the Pleasure Hall owned by <a href="/wiki/Black_Maria" title="Black Maria">Black Maria</a>. Carrot, Shinobu, and Nami volunteered to go look for Momonosuke.<sup id="cite_ref-159" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After they separated from Kin'emon's forces and the Brachio Tank V, they ran into <a href="/wiki/Prometheus" title="Prometheus">Prometheus</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup> The three quickly fled from the homie as it called Big Mom.<sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup> However, Carrot, Nami, and Zeus were later captured and taken to the Live Stage.<sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> When Big Mom encountered Luffy during the raid, Nami and Carrot freed themselves from the homies holding them, as Nami used her Sorcery Clima-Tact and Carrot used the Electro-based attack Eleclaw.<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png/revision/latest?cb=20230715142052" class="image"><img alt="Perospero Defeats Carrot and Wanda" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Perospero Defeats Carrot and Wanda.png" data-image-key="Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230715142052" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png/revision/latest?cb=20230715142052" class="image"><img alt="Perospero Defeats Carrot and Wanda" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230715142052" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Perospero Defeats Carrot and Wanda.png" data-image-key="Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/be/Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20230715142052" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Perospero_Defeats_Carrot_and_Wanda.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot and Wanda are defeated by Perospero.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Carrot spotted <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> and Perospero meeting with Big Mom, she decided to go after Perospero to avenge Pedro's death.<sup id="cite_ref-c992_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c992-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> After transforming into their Sulong forms, Carrot and Wanda attacked Perospero and wounded him.<sup id="cite_ref-c995_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c995-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Despite their incredible power, Carrot and Wanda were defeated after they lost their Sulong transformation when the moon got covered by clouds.<sup id="cite_ref-c1006_43-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1006-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> After the two recovered later, they spotted the Sulong-transformed <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a> arrive to fight Perospero.<sup id="cite_ref-c1023_44-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1023-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> Though they were worried when the storm clouds blocked off the full moon causing Nekomamushi to revert back and get badly injured by Perospero, once the clouds parted due to the clashing of advanced-grade <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, Nekomamushi was able to regain his Sulong form and swiftly defeated Perospero with <i>Oden One Sword Style: Neko Niko Ban</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-c1026_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1026-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After this she goes to hug Nekomamushi, where he tells her to be careful not to transform into sulong because the moon has been seen again.<sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> Suddenly, <a href="/wiki/Onigashima" title="Onigashima">Onigashima</a> begins to move, so she, Nekomamushi, and Wanda decide to head back to the castle so they do not fall.<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> Once inside, they joined the resurging battle against the Beasts Pirates, who once again started to fight the Alliance's forces.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png/revision/latest?cb=20240821123232" class="image"><img alt="Mokomo Dukedom Celebrates in Wano" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mokomo Dukedom Celebrates in Wano.png" data-image-key="Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240821123232" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png/revision/latest?cb=20240821123232" class="image"><img alt="Mokomo Dukedom Celebrates in Wano" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240821123232" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mokomo Dukedom Celebrates in Wano.png" data-image-key="Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ad/Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20240821123232" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mokomo_Dukedom_Celebrates_in_Wano.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Carrot celebrates Wano's victory with the rest of the Mokomo Dukedom.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the raid concluded, Carrot was among the the spectators in the alliance watching Kouzuki Momonosuke being announced as the next Shogun of Wano. Carrot was smiling at the news of Momo now becoming the shogun.<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> A week later, after Luffy and Zoro finally woke up, Carrot joined the other women in a bath<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> and later she joined in celebrating the festival in the Flower Capital.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the festival, while she was eating, Carrot was informed by both Inuarashi and Nekomamushi that they were stepping down from their positions as the rulers of the <a href="/wiki/Mokomo_Dukedom" title="Mokomo Dukedom">Mokomo Dukedom</a> to remain in Wano and had decided to appoint Carrot as the next ruler due to her previous journey with the Sanji Retrieval Team and her experience of seeing the world being necessary for the new era. Though Carrot was shocked by this decision, as there were other minks more qualified than her, the two reminded her that she possesses the same <a href="/wiki/Inherited_Will" title="Inherited Will">will</a> that Pedro once had.<sup id="cite_ref-c1056_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1056-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the new ruler of the Mokomo Dukedom, Carrot was seen listening to <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s broadcast with her fellow mink friends, showing amazement at the advanced technology of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Kingdom" title="Great Kingdom">ancient kingdom</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup><br style="clear:both;" />
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>During the escape from Whole Cake Island in the anime, Carrot defeated <a href="/wiki/Charlotte_Tablet" title="Charlotte Tablet">Tablet</a> in the Seducing Woods.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup> In the manga, the entire pursuit squad was defeated by Nami using Zeus' thunderbolt.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>The nickname that Carrot had given to Chopper, "Choniki" (a combination of the words "Chopper" and "brother"), has been translated as "Chobro" in the English version.</li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FCarrot%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li>Carrot's favorite food is the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carrot" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Carrot">vegetable</a> she's named after follows a popular misconception about rabbits,<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> most famously depicted with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bugs_Bunny" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Bugs Bunny">Bugs Bunny</a>. In real life, carrots can actually make rabbits sick. They normally eat leafy vegetables such as cabbage, kale, or just grass.
<ul><li>Additionally, Carrot is shown to love chocolate, which is just as bad, if not worse for rabbits in real life.</li>
<li>Strangely, she has also been seen eating meat, something rabbits cannot do due to their herbivorous diet. She also appeared to have some knowledge about fish due to knowing about the nature of carp, which indicates that she has eaten fish before.</li></ul></li>
<li>Carrot's general behavior is stereotypical of rabbits: in addition to her preference for the vegetable of the same name, she also likes to be petted on the head, an action normally done to pet rabbits, and has a very energetic and bouncy personality similar to the agitated nature of real life rabbits, as these animals need ample space to move and play.</li>
<li>Despite being a member of <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi" title="Inuarashi">Inuarashi</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Inuarashi_Musketeer_Squad" title="Inuarashi Musketeer Squad">Musketeers</a>, Carrot wears a green cape, a signature item of <a href="/wiki/Nekomamushi" title="Nekomamushi">Nekomamushi</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Guardians" title="Guardians">Guardians</a>.
<ul><li>This is probably due to her training under <a href="/wiki/Pedro" title="Pedro">Pedro</a>, a Guardian, rather than <a href="/wiki/Shishilian" title="Shishilian">Shishilian</a>, a Musketeer.</li></ul></li>
<li>Carrot is the second person to stowaway on a <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Straw Hat ship</a>.</li>
<li>Carrot was ranked 26th and 8th place in the sixth and seventh <a href="/wiki/Popularity_Polls" title="Popularity Polls">popularity polls</a> respectively, making her the most popular member of the Mink Tribe and the fourth most popular female character.</li>
<li>Carrot's birthday, May 24, comes from a fan suggestion: 5 from meal<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ごはん</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji"><b>Go</b>han</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, 2 from carrot<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">にんじん</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji"><b>Ni</b>njin</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> and 4 from white rabbit<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">白ウサギ</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji"><b>Shi</b>ro Usagi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-birth_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-birth-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
